The first method involves making three or four cauterisations in a line along the length of the mouse, following the shape of the liver cautery we described earlier; do not press your hand on the entire cautery, and have the patient lean over their back; another cautery method is to heat up the iron with two nerves, as we showed for shoulder dislocation; lift up the heart which is at the site of the mouse, or where the patient's pain comes from towards the left, and let the elevation by which you lift the heart follow the length of the body, and let the cautery follow the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, 
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After treatment, when it has thrown up pus for a long time, this is worse than other treatments mentioned earlier.
de ydropisie	Of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not effective for dropsy, except in the manner called 'ascites'.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods we have mentioned in the divisions, and your treatment does not benefit them, then you must make four cauterizations around the navel, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back on the spine, and one near the breasts; and let the cauterizations be close to the heart's base.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	Afterwards, leave the open cauterization for a long time to drain pus, and do not let go of the patient's treatment after cauterization; healing would quicken, and the two intentions would come together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The form of the cautery for the belly should be as we have shown before with the clavicle; and that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what has been stated previously.
de l’enfleure des piez	Of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical, and they are full of yellow water, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger; lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go in too deeply, otherwise you would burn the yellow water, and the cautery should be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After that, make two cauteries on each leg at the tip of the little finger; and let the long cauteries be one beneath the knee in front and the other outside, in the middle of the leg; leave the cauteries without cleaning them for a long time so that the yellow water comes out; after treating the other conditions we have mentioned.
de la menoison	Of the household
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the abdominal illness comes from cold and moisture, such that the retaining and digestive virtues in the stomach and intestine are weakened, and it cannot be cured by regular treatments; you see the patient suffering greatly with strong vitality, then perform a large circular cautery on the stomach as described before for the stomach cautery; four small subtle cauteries around the navel along with one larger subtle cautery, and two more cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, perform a cautery on the wrist, one cautery on each elbow, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When hemorrhoids are present at the foundation (anus), whether one or multiple, and they are old, consisting of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and treatment as previously mentioned in divisions is not beneficial, then cauterization is performed: III on the spine of the back, which is entirely outside the lower abdomen area, with three triangular-shaped cauterizations; I cautery beneath the buttocks for two days. If you suspect their stomach has become cold, and food is not being digested properly, causing the face to swell, then apply I large cautery on the stomach as previously mentioned, and I other cautery on the liver (liver), and I another on the spleen, with all three cauterizations clavi-shaped; leave the cautery open for a long period of time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, let the wound heal completely.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of fleshiness which is called 'thelul'
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat the 'thelul', heat up the cautery like a razor, then place it fully ablaze on top of the treated 'thelul'; leave your hand there until the cautery touches the edge of the wound, from which blood flows; do this once or twice, and if there is more 'thelul', cauterise each one as we have said; afterward treat with healing ointments until they are healed; and if you cauterise with a large cautery on 'alchatim', it will provide greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of wound poorly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When a patient cannot endure cutting or opening, as we will explain in their place, such illness arises that can only be healed by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a certain person develops a fistula, and it becomes infested with worms and corrupted moisture, you should treat it with an entire delicate dressing, making sure you know the entire extent of the wound.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cauterizing iron like a razor, insert it into the fistula according to how deep the dressing is, and repeat the cautery as many times as needed until all corrupted flesh is burned away, once or twice or thrice depending on need; be careful not to burn any nerves or major veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; 
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease.
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain from coldness comes to the kidneys, and there is severe flatulence, and it does not take on a female appearance, then you must perform cautery on the kidneys, one on each side, with the clavicle cautery we mentioned before; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauteries in a line, and they will provide greater relief.
de la vessie	Of bladder disease.
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak due to coldness and moisture, such that the patient retains urine, then perform cautery outside on the part where the hair begins on the forearm, one on each side, each cautery as long as a thumb's width; and do one cautery outside the back, or two if needed; and let the clavicle cauteries be done according to the form mentioned before.
de la marris	From illness
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their endings delayed; and when they come, she feels great pain: then it is necessary to perform three cauterizations around the navel, as we have said for bladder cautery, and two cauterizations outside the back; and let the cauterization be claviated, as we have explained.
de la hainche	Of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When viscous moistures descend into the hip joint, and due to this it moves out of its place, and the sign is that one thigh appears longer than the other when measured together; and if you find the area of separation below, then you must cauterize the patient on the hip joint with one cautery resembling a circle, and bleed in front of the location around the joint as it turns, so that the joint remains within the circle; and let this cautery be similar to that used for the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cautery is not present, make three large olive branch cauteries, and let the cauterization be as perfect as all hearts; and treat until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	From the pain in the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the hip joint, caused by cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated as we have said in the division but is not cured, and the illness is chronic: then you must purge the patient of thick foul humors with fetid pills or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After performing the cautery; and the method of cauterization is in two ways: that is to say, with burning medicines or with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Cautery of fire is practiced in many ways, one of which is as follows: make three triangular cauterizations over the bone of the hip, in this shape; make them deep and wide; leave space between each one equal to the width of a thumb; let the cauterizations be olive-shaped. Sometimes it is done in the center, on top of the head of the hip; therefore, there are four of them made according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you prefer, use the circular cautery we described earlier for hip dislocations; but make it so that the circles encompass the entire hip, and all heartwood is burnt.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	This method is used for sciatica when the pain remains in the hip and does not extend down to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	Et if it comes down to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations where the patient says the pain is located, and four cauterizations above the ankle on the left side slightly; let the cauterization be cutellary, burning off the thickest part of the heart; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to the toes or nearby, cauterize it three times with a point or four times with a 'point' cauterizer.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if necessary, do more; and if you know that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, make a cutellary or circular cauterization, and be careful with all your cauterizations not to leave them too long so as not to burn nerves and large arteries, and cause greater harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who underwent fire cauterization on the ankle of their foot, and they left it until the leg was entirely swollen, as well as the feet, and [their] feet were pierced and corrupted altogether.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an evacuation of his belly, from which he had death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, cauterize in one part and in the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise ones said about cauterization of the hip, that this is how it should be done: make such an iron tool and have its head as big as a two-digit measure or a little less, and between the prongs, which are intertwined, let there be space equal to one thumb width; and the prongs shall go in one side and end on another with their tips facing outwards from each other by two parts, and there should also be handles made of iron well crafted; this is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And heat it until it is all red and throw away the coals, then put it on top of the sick hip bone and rotate to the painful side; cauterize once with one iron and leave for three days; afterwards apply an ointment plaster, leaving the wound open a long time; after the cure of ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says we use this cautery sparingly due to the fear of its appearance, and see little who do so; yet it is a good cauterization, which can be endured where there is need for it.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The burning cautery of medicine is such that you make one instrument made up of crossed pieces into which the margin of a door fits, and it is either brass or iron on one side long, and in height has two nails, and between each there is the quantity of the thickness of a finger; and they are open below and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After place the box of the hip on the patient lying on their sound side, and press your hand mightily upon the box of the hip; thereafter pour between the two circles of hot water that has been heated over one fire pot, and leave it an hour's time, and let the patient suffer its heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it shall find cauterization akin to fire there, and once the cauterization is passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip with gentle water, and leave thus three days, and apply butter until that which is black from the scalding has been removed; and let this stand for three days while putrefaction is extracted; and this would be the final aid after the cure of ointments so long as it heals.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or down to the leg, make an instrument for him that holds salt according to what you have done at the hip similarly; and this is the manner of the hot compress, and I have written about it in the treatise on medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, equal parts of each, grind them together, and place them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	where there is a small opening for the entry of a razor's point; place this pot inside another well-sealed one, and add alkali, quicklime, and warm water above it, enough so that two fingers are covered when you grasp it by hand; let it sit until cool water and vapor descend into the sealed pot, then take all this water and pour it back over the alkali and quicklime as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And so it will be very painful and treated in many ways through medical practices and cauteries of other members. For fire produces a similar effect to them, and there are other medicines that cauterize the hip just as well, such as tesysey, honey, anacardium nut oil, and hot soap; all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment where a man was cured of hip pain and sciatic nerve pain, he suffered greatly, and says no other treatment was done, and that he was healed in one go when this treatment was performed; and it is as follows.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he says to do it in this way: take some fresh and dry verdigris litharge, and grind it very well with one part of fat, then place it on the hip, thigh, and leg where the pain is; and bind it there. Leave it for three hours or as much time as the patient does not feel a burning sensation anymore.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then have him enter the bath until his body is slightly warmed up, and make him go to bed, and the pain will disappear completely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicinal cauterization without first evacuating the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat dung, it greatly helps; and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take some linen and smear it with old oil, and apply it to the hollow between the big toe and the one next to it, called the fossa.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Then take dry goat dung and light it until it becomes charcoal, put it on the linen, and leave it there until it goes out; repeat this process again and keep doing so without stopping until you think by feeling that it reaches up to the hip, and the pain has ceased; and this type of cautery is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether due to falling, impact, excessive bleeding, or similar matters involving cold and dispersed material, cauterization is effective only for that which arises from an influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	One must then ensure the patient is purged of fetid pills or other similar substances, applying three rows of signed enamel to the back where pain persists, with five cauterizations per row based on virtue and quantity that the patient can withstand; perform these cauterizations using the "pin" method, but if preferred, one may use four at the median cleat instead, arranged thusly:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This illness often afflicts young children, and the initial signs include a constricted collarbone upon rising, accompanied by fear; one finds an appearance in the lower spine region of the back, similar to that observed elsewhere.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this one and wish to treat it, cauterize it with a hot iron according to this method.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery touches each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish to do so, circumferentially cauterize the spine with a hot iron in two or three lines close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treating the area until it is healed as we have said, take care not to apply a hot iron to any spinal nerve or its surroundings.
de la dolor des jointes	On the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When joint pain is caused by moisture spread to each limb of the body, and when it presents in the foot, which physicians call "gout", and when it is due to cold and cannot be cured with medicine, then it should be treated with cautery in this manner: make several cauterizations around the ankle joint, and let the cauteries have an olive shape according to this pattern:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need to grasp onto the face of the foot, perform a 'point' cauterization on it.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	If the pains reach up to the knees and other joints, and this happens frequently, perform three or four 'olive' cauterizations on each knee, for each part; if you need more, do more but do not hold your hand there once the heart's steel is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, administer the cauterization we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	If the pains are in the hands, make 'points' around the wrist with two lines; if there is no pain remaining in the arms, make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand; if the pains reach up to the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and ensure good care for the patient and provide medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good treatment and purge the phlegm, he will recover with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the fracture of the thighbone.
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When fracture happens in the groin area, and the balls descend into the scrotum, if it is recent, you should ensure that he does not urinate that day when you treat him. Let him take things which ease the belly, so that urine passes from his stomach. After this make him sit on his back between your hands, tell him to hold his breath until the balls are returned to their place and draw them with your fingers. Then cut over the fracture site above the bone of the wrist, and in all a sign that is similar to half a circle across the body; then heat up this cautery which has this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as they are white and give off no odor.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Realign the balls to their place; and have your assistant hold his hand still so that it doesn't return backward; and work well on the patient's thighs, and place a cushion underneath him with a strap over the thighs, and another one holding his hands; then apply the cautery right up to your whole hand, and keep it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, repeat again until you come up to the bone; and be careful that the ball doesn't pop out when you are doing the cautery; or else you'll burn him; and because of this, the patient might die, or suffer other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you don't reach the bone with the cautery, your work is useless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And the cautery for children should be subtle according to their size, and for adults also large according to their measure; after III days treat the place of the cautery with butter until the scald is removed; after that cure other ointments so it heals, and let the patient lie on his back XL days until the wound is well-fused; and make sure their nourishment is satisfying over a long period, so the belly doesn't protrude when he tries to get up.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After XL days, when he wishes to rise, provide him with a well-made bandage, and wear it for another XL days; let him have good rest, do not work hard nor overfill his belly, nor shout too much; and once he follows this instruction, he will be fully healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	Et I shall say hereafter the cure of cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	De the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other bellies and are known, and you see that they no longer grow, if it is the first cautery, make it according to its quantity, and burn one third of the heart; afterward, treat it as we have said; and some ancients say that it must be cauterized with a three-angled cautery in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the place of attachment and make a line across the width above the rupture, then another outside it; hold your hand in the middle of the entire cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and quicker.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any limb, whether from a fall or an injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it is necessary that they be cauterized with the cautery called "point," and the cautery should be applied according to the length of the limb, its thickness, weakness, strength, and the location of twists and pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cautery is effective, it is good; if not, apply another cautery on top of it, for it is customary that it must move to the member closest to it, which means you should perform cauteries until the patient is cured.
de meselerie	of surgery
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The months are aided sometimes by cautery with great relief, especially for illnesses that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you want to see the patient cauterized, be careful if it is at the beginning of their illness and if they are treated as we have said in the previous division, and do not decrease nor stay still, but you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the disease; then make five cauterizations on top of the head: one in the middle of the scalp to the nape of the neck, another towards the front at the end of the hairline, and two more on each side; finally, one behind on the highest point. Leave your hand there until you reach the bone and as long as scabs form so that vapors from thick humours can escape; cauterize it like this under the skin.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	Et si le mal est partout dispersé ; et qu'elle perd manifestement, alors il convient que tu la cautérises avec ces cautères que nous avons dit pour le chef, et un cautère sur le nez, et deux cautères sur l'épine du cou, et six cautères sur l'épine du dos, et un grand sur la crupie et un autre à côté, et deux sur les deux épaules ; et deux sur les coudes, et deux sur les tendons du poignet, et un sur chaque joint des mains et des pieds, et sur les creux des mains ; et garde-toi des nerfs qui sont sur l'arrière en marchant, que tu ne les brûles ; et quelquefois fais un cautère sur l'os du poignet, et un autre sur l'os de l'estomac, et un autre sur le foie.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the more you perform cauterization, the more help it provides and benefits them; and know that patients feel no pain from the cautery as healthy people do because their bodies are already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	The cautery should be large or small depending on the limbs and joints, according to what you find in terms of iron tools.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment apply flour paste to the place, mixed with honey and other treatments until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicine, oils, and poultices but it is not healed, then apply cautery to the affected limb according to its size, let the cautery be a little inside towards the heart; then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And sometimes one performs cauterization on the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is removed; yet still none should attempt this if they are not knowledgeable about limbs and the paths of moving nerves.
de albaras	From whitlows
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called 'whitlows' persists and medicinal remedies are ineffective, cauterize it with a moderate cautery, according to the species of the heart's quantity, until the white is removed, and its color changes; then treat it with a mixture of flour from vetch and lentils along with rose oil and plantain leaves, and blood from pigeons and doves, each in equal parts; blend everything together, apply as a poultice to the affected area, and let it air until healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of cancer by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer arises at the beginning, and you wish to halt its progress, cauterize it with a circular-shaped cautery, all around the circumference of the cancerous growth.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And yet the wise physicians say that one should also cauterize the center of the cancerous growth; however, this does not seem good to me, for I fear it may become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen this happen several times before; a more proper approach is to cauterize around its edges, with the circular-shaped cautery, as we have discussed previously in regard to various types of cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	On swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When one has an illness called "adubelati", and it delays death either due to its excessiveness or because of the patient's water when they are decrepit (that is, very old) and have little blood, or because of the season; and you see that it hastens their death: then cauterize them with many small cauteries by pricking; afterwards leave them be.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten their death.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through the entire cautery, heat the cautery with what it is made of:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	Place your hand over the middle of this illness called "adubelati" until the cautery has pierced the heart, and let these cauteries be such that the patient feels them from the outside in such a way as to alleviate the course of the putrefaction.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment, ensure it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cautery with iron  tool
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another type of illness there is which is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than the wasting away of limbs, for it gnaws at the limbs just as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this illness in a place that can withstand fire cautery, then heat up small and large iron tools according to what is suitable for the location of the disease; afterwards cauterize it thoroughly from all sides until you eradicate any corruption, leaving nothing of it behind so that everything that was corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and apply ground up herbs with oil to the cauterized areas until the burns from the fire are gone along with all of the corrupted tissue.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of ointments generates flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy flesh has not formed, it is good; and if not, restart the cautery on what remains of the corrupted tissue.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this treatment has sometimes been cured with medical ointment instead of fire cautery; however, fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already explained the cure with medical ointment in the relevant section: take whichever you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	from boils that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often there is a disease that occurs on the feet called "claws" in our terminology, and it is a faulty, swollen thing that wounds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization for this illness is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, cauterization by fire, and cauterization with hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Cauterization by fire is when you heat a hollow cautery like a quill, made of good iron sized to fit over the nail from all sides and with fine edges; after placing it hot over the nail, turn your hand around the nail until it reaches its base; leave it there for three days until it begins to discharge pus; then apply a plaster of wild mallows ground with salt, leaving the plaster on overnight, and the nail will fall out, uprooted from its root.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Cure the wound's place of treatment with ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by fire into the body, and often occur on hands and feet, then you must apply hot water cautery; it is done in this way: take a brass or iron rod, or a pigeon feather, and place it over the wart and touch it with a nail, that is, for treating warts; put the rod on so that it grips all around, then add a drop of hot water, hold your hand steady, and press your hand in rotation so that the edge of the rod reaches the root of the wart, allowing the hot water to penetrate deep down to the root; let the patient bear the stinging sensation of the hot water for an hour; then leave it be, and it will remove all roots altogether.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another, until you have reset all those that are out of joint in the body, then treat them with ointments that produce flesh.
li cure dou trembler	the doctor for shaking (or trembling)
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When someone shakes from coldness of nerves, or from quartan fever or another, you should apply four cauterizations, or five, along the spine of the back, one between each vertebra; and one on the foot, and one on the stomach using an olive-oil cautery; this will stop the shaking and hasten recovery from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	smelly blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes the body breaks out in baths (sores) or smelly blisters, which come from gross corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	So it is suitable at first when they appear that one should perform a cautery on each head of the pustule: a subtle cautery with myrtle wood, so that the tip is taken by fire, or with the root of long aristoloche, or with the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And sometimes one cauterizes them at the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and they cannot grow further, but rather the excess from which they come is destroyed, and they are healed; but it should be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut.
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	There are often great outpourings of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound which comes afterwards, or when incising an abscess, or with a member's cauterization, and in similar things; it is very difficult to stop this bleeding.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And nevertheless when it happens to someone, hurry up and place your index finger on the wound's injury, press hard so that the blood is calmed beneath your finger, with no more drops escaping; then put several small and large olive oil cauterizers over fire until they are all red; take one, big or small depending on the wound and where the artery goes, and place the cauterizer above said vein while you hold your finger down, keeping the cauterizer there until bleeding stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it should burst open when you lift your finger from the wound, and the cauterizers are cold, take another one quickly from those that are over fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	Do not cease doing one after the other until bleeding stops; be careful that you do not burn the nearby nerve, nor any other harm come to the patient; know that when blood flows from an artery, it cannot be properly staunched especially if the artery is large, unless by one of four methods we have mentioned: either by cauterization, or by extraction if it has not been treated, or by strong binding with thread, or by applying medicines that can stop bleeding; and bind and tighten appropriately.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers restraint with a tightly wrapped bandage of fine cloth or places hot objects on it, or similar treatments, may not find them beneficial.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to someone and they do not have a doctor or medicine available, then they must place their index finger on the wound over the vein as mentioned before, and press down firmly until it is compressed above the wound and the vein; without moving the finger, moisten it with cold water often, ensuring it is very cold so that the blood becomes solidified and thickened and compressed; afterwards, make arrangements for what they require in terms of cauterisation and medication.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book on surgical procedures.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We told you in the first chapter about all illnesses that require cauterisation with fire or burning medications and their various applications, causes, instruments and forms; I placed this chapter on the head to feet so that one can more easily find what they are looking for.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so when I begin this, my dear child, you must learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the previous one on cauterization, and therefore it requires even greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many different kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	They come with such fear and awareness of their illness that they die easily from the shock of encountering their disease and the severity of their condition; these are the ones we must fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And there are those who give you their sense, and say: "Wait, I am healed"; and yet the illness is deceitful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	You should not agree to those who come to you with such claims, but put greater concern in your honor than in your greed, and do not act foolishly but wisely in matters of which you are certain and can obtain profit from; use prognostication and indication in treating your patients for their benefit; this will help you gain a good reputation, glory, and honorable memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, may our Lord give you good understanding and guidance, and if he wishes, inspire you with his holy breath of spirit, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter for you in a way that divides it into sections, according to how it stands before the chapter on cauterization, which I explained to you from head to toe, so that you can find more easily what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	Head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this illness often comes to children at birth when the midwife grasps the child's head too tightly; and sometimes it happens for reasons unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this illness occur in anyone but children, and all those whom I have seen suffer from it have died; for that reason, I think it is best to leave such treatment to others.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child whose shoulder was full of water, and the head grew larger each day until he could no longer bear it; and the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture had gathered beneath the bone on the side of the spine, between the heart and the bone; and the treatment is such if the moisture is between the heart and bone, and the abscesses are small, that you must make an incision into the head a breadth of two fingers long so that the moisture flows out; and here is the form of the spatulum:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper, and the abscesses are larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see signs of the sutures of the head opening on each side, and the water springs forth when you press it with your hand from within, and this does not stop: then you must make three incisions into the head in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all moisture vigorously.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After applying compresses and powders, bind it with wine and oil, leaving it thus for five days; then release the binding, treat the wound with dressings and ointments, keep the head in an even position, and feed the patient dry meat to avoid moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	Another manner of incision is when you observe where the swelling and collection of pus are visible; sometimes it is in front, at other times behind, to the right or left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Make an incision at the site of visible pus and swelling, opening it up according to your ability; take care not to cut the artery; and if blood flows, let the patient bleed from this loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of rheumatism
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it happens to someone that they suffer from a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or throat, and this disease is chronic, and medical treatment provides no benefit, then the last resort is cautery along with cutting of the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Therefore, when you are about to cut the veins, have the patient lean back; afterward, rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries become visible, then restrain the patient's neck with a cloth; look where the vein passes, and how it lies between one and the other ear, and press upon it; cauterize these areas first, then cut both of them with an acute spatule to the bone, and do this across the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see it, push the spatula under the artery and flip the piece above, cutting as deep as necessary across it.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	When the vein is cut open, blood will continuously gush out in a torrent.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If the artery does not open to bleeding, you must measure out a length of three fingers' breadth and incise down to the bone; the amount of blood that will flow is six half-ounces, perhaps slightly more or less depending on how much the patient can endure and according to how full the artery is; then inspect the wound: if any part remains above the bone without being cauterized by a hot iron, reopen the wound so abscesses do not form; afterward extract any foreign bodies and bind the wound with bandages, treating it until completely healed.
de emigrainne	Of a migraine.
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes with a cold and moisture in the eyes, hot temples, recurring headaches from long ago, and similar issues; if medicines, cures, and other treatments do not help, we remove the arteries of the temples and cauterize them, as we have explained.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is such that the patient should pluck the hairs from their temples and pay attention to the artery which appears in the temple, for it shows itself clearly through its pulsation, being more prominent in some men who are very cold; if it is hidden, then the patient should wrap his neck with some cloth, then rub the place with a rough fabric and moisten it with hot water until the artery becomes plainly visible; take this instrument whose form is as follows:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then pull it upwards with pincers, and separate well the membranes that are underneath on each side; and if the artery is subtle, turn it to the point of the probe, then cut it from this part according to the quantity of the two edges.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, the blood cannot flow out entirely from all over.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And drain the blood from the six cavities until only three remain; and if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread, so that pus does not come out before the wound heals, and blood continues to flow; then cut away the surplus between the two ties at the same time, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with the knife-cauterizer until the edges are cut through to the bone; and this is a dangerous operation if the patient does not have a fever and has a hot complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For cauterization is helpful to dry out moisture, it is of great aid for such moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	Where it is necessary for the extraction of arteries to fill the space with old cotton and place well-made bandages on top; and when you remove them, ensure you use dry medicines that promote flesh growth, and bandages, until it heals; and if blood escapes from the artery while you work, then quickly cut it off with cauterization, or use vitriol and squeeze it in your hand to stop the bleeding; and if you don't have those available, put your finger over the wound until the blood coagulates, pour cold water on the area to stem the flow, and ensure it is tightly bound as needed; what is harmful and more dangerous during artery extraction is that you cauterize the vein with this sharp cautery in two parts, but make sure the incisions are deep enough to retain heat for longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too thin, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And there should be a width of one finger between the two blades, and then when you have clamped down on the two places, place the burning iron onto it until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein into two parts; and let them be separated between the two shoulders because this cautery is not continuous throughout. And this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears from the eyes flow down onto the veins that are on top of the head from fire, and it does not help to treat with medicine what is done there, and you see the patient's face turn red, and feel trembling on the forehead; and their eyes become thin and moist so that the hairs of the eyelids fall out, and the eyelids are scalded by the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», and it is that you do at the back of the patient who has this disease, the hair on his forehead; then make three incisions on his forehead evenly along the length of his forehead; one incision should be like two fingers wide in the middle of his forehead going downwards to his nose; the other two are located above each temple, and you must avoid cutting into the arteries which are found at each side above the temples; move your hand away from where the two jaws connect, and let each wound have a length of three finger widths across, horizontally; have ready a piece of sponge and much cloth without holes to wipe the blood, then insert the sharp spatule in two parts of which this is formed:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; and remove all the skin that is between the two incisions down to the bone, then do likewise from the middle incision to the other second one, and afterwards extract this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	So push the instrument called "scalpel" into the first incision; it is very sharp on one side and soft, not sharp, on the other, and this is its shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the sharp side toward the flesh near the heart and the soft side towards the bone; push it until it reaches the middle incision.
