Cela se produit à cause de l'extension de la fistule qui est dans l'aine, comme nous l'avons dit, car elle s'étend et devient molle ; la peau se détend et s'ouvre en raison de cette extension. Le traitement consiste alors en un cautère, comme nous l'avons mentionné auparavant, mais il existe aussi une autre méthode : le patient est souvent couché sur le dos entre tes mains ; ensuite tu incises la zone autour de la rupture, qui est gonflée sur les trois côtés, et retires la fistule qui se trouve sous la peau ; ensuite tu prends un fer et l'appliques à cet endroit ; puis tu coupes la première et la seconde couche de peau qui sont apparentes sur le dessus du fer, puis tu enlèves le bout du fer sans rien couper autour de la plaie ni rien étirer, comme je te l'ai déjà fait savoir pour le traitement de la rupture intestinale ; ensuite on traite la plaie.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you treat the wound, clean it thoroughly and heal the injury so it is restored to health.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The incision is constricted, and there is no visible appearance of the fracture, and cauterization is suitable in this place, being closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of softening the tough skin on the calves
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Often the tough skin on the calves is softened in some people because the tendons within are weakened and it is visible; and when one wants to treat it, they must make the patient lie on their back, and then cut away the softened skin from the natural skin underneath; then bring together the two lips into a suture, and if you wish, stitch away the superfluous part of the softened skin with three or four firm stitches; then cut between the sutures, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	Chastity.
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You know that chastity is forbidden in our law, and for this reason, I would prefer not to discuss it in this book; and it is necessary for two reasons: one being that the surgeon should be able to answer when asked about it, and know its cure; the other is because we often need to castrate certain animals to aid us, such as goats, sheep, cattle, and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say therefore that castration is performed in two ways: either by attraction or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In the method we perform by attraction, we make the animal sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and hanging; then take them with your hand, holding them gently so they are released and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphrodites are according to two manners among men: one is that between the two testicles appears also like the figure of a woman's nature, where there is hair, and sometimes urine comes out.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is in women, and it has on the wrist also like a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	And the treatment for men and women is that you join together all the flesh, and treat it like other wounds; in the second manner, for men whose urine passes through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	Of the contagion.
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	Tentigene is a flesh-adorned part of the natural body, so ugly to behold; and some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	You must hold the excess of tentigene in your hand or somewhere nearby, and lightly scrape it; do not go too deep, lest blood flow forth, then cure with another cure until it is healed; and to another part that grows at the mouth of the wound, remove it, and perhaps it will be gone, and it appears like a cow, thus the ancients called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	You must scrape it, as we said for tentigene, and cure until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	Erratic is when the nature of the woman's passage is not perceived or is small; and it is natural by birth, or accidental due to illness that has developed; or it is through an attached chariot, or a subtle device made from silk or similar material, and it exists within the uterus, or on its sides, or underneath, wherever it may be; and it prevents conception, childbirth, and possibly menstruation; and this condition is recognized by observing the discharge.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the obstruction is visible nearby, reach for it with your fingers or with forceps.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	If it is a device made from silk or similar material and is close to the two lips, act quickly like this: put your two index fingers together, have the woman lie on her back with legs spread; then stretch open the two lips so that you can see the subtle device and move it past the obstruction; then take wool, dip it in oil, and place it where the device was, and make sure the woman stays at home each day until it does not heal over.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the tumor is hard and thick, you must cut it with a spatoula resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the obstruction is of recent birth, suspend it with a hook and cut it; and have medicines that stop bleeding, such as dragon's blood, incense, mixed with egg white; then apply a wide lead cane so that the wound cannot close; thus let it be long-lasting, and bring him a dressing of dry linen; then treat other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when recent flesh appears in the marrow, it must be cut according to this method, unless it is deep-rooted abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For the deep-rooted abscess in the marrow, one must not apply cauterization.
des emorroides	The hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood usually flows out, and when hemorrhoids become old, they turn into boils; we have mentioned their similarities elsewhere, along with the signs, and I will now tell you those that can be cured.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and boils, when they are perfectly even in the flesh and do not appear to the touch, cannot be cured with iron instruments.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the flesh, which can be felt, are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	You must therefore put the woman in a cold house, then stretch the boil with pincers and cut it at its root; then apply powder made of medicines that restrain bleeding, such as dragon's blood and frankincense and similar things; then have her feet against the wall for an hour, after which you put her in cold water; if any more blood comes out, make her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate rind, gallnuts and similar things, then take barley flour and mix it with honey and egg white to form a plaster which is applied on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops bleeding, it is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	If it does not stop, make him bleed by applying cups to his back and breasts without causing injury; then take linen, soak it in the juice of plantain or hawthorn with old wine, and apply it to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the abscess subsides, treat the area with ointment until it heals; and this one called "albathir" is red, similar to rough skin on a head, so you must cut it as I said for "thelul", and then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	abscesses of the womb
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscess come from the womb, such as cancer, stony abscess, herpes, cysts, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in this chapter.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	It is necessary then that I speak in this treatise of the hot abscess that appears on the buttocks, which is not one of the abscesses that fall under surgery; and if you wish to know the treatment for iron, look to see if the abscess has grown quickly from its beginning, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	So do not hasten to pierce it, but let it die until the pain is eased; and then make the patient sit on a seat, and have two small stools for them to lean on, supporting their back and bringing their feet up to outside of their legs; and let their thighs be spread apart, and put their arms underneath their knees, and bind them well with a good bandage; then suck it out towards the right side, and apply the instrument used to open the mouth of the abscess, from which hereafter comes its shape; and when you wish to apply this instrument, you must first mark out a line to know the depth of the abscess, so that what goes into the instrument doesn't go too deep inside it should not hurt the patient; and if the instrument is larger, then cover the bottom of the abscess with cloth, so that the instrument does not injure them; and let him hold the horn of the instrument on top, while you hold the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.	And when the abscess opens up, and you treat it with soft hands, you must cut it at its head, or let it burst on its own accord; once the pus is expelled from within, you should apply moistened bandages soaked in rose oil, or dry bandages soaked in green oil; place the moistened bandage underneath the wound directly against the abscess, and place a clean woolen cloth on top of the abscess and the wound, which has been dampened with water or cooked with mallow leaves; treat it after two days of this poultice until it is healed; and sometimes you should wash the abscess and the wound with warm water and honey, then again with water or roots of lilies and long aristologhe, before returning to the poultice.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is swollen in the abscess, you must be careful not to cauterize with iron, but treat it as we have said in the section on wounds.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	The first duty at the birth is for her to know the shape of natural childbirth, and its signs are when you see the woman pressing down, and wanting to smell air: then the child hastens to come out quickly; thus, you know that these births are according to nature, with the issue coming from above his head, and the midwife assists him; and when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press on her belly so that the child comes out soon; because as he descends towards his head, so does the midwife assist him, and the woman expels her superfluities through a good delivery; and those who come otherwise do not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	For sometimes it comes out from his feet or shoulders and hands, or he may come out belly down, often with head turned towards his collarbone, or in other bad shapes; thus, it is the duty of the midwife to be wise and clever about these things, taking care of errors and disappointments, and I will show you all possible shapes how one must assist her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the child is born on its head by natural delivery, and the woman labours greatly while birthing, and her strength is weak, then let her sit on a saddle or be held by women; and stimulate her nature with oil from fenugreek that has been cooked, and then insert the small spatula of this form between her two breasts:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Then split the amniotic sac and trim her nails down to their quick so that the fluids flow out; press on her belly so that the child descends, and if it does not descend, then administer an enema of fenugreek powder with sesame oil; make her sneeze by applying condy's crystals to her nose and mouth, and hold her there for one hour: thus draw forth the child.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if both hands emerge first, you must pull them back lightly one at a time; and if they cannot be drawn in, then place the woman on a chair, lifting her feet upwards; stand up the chair from the ground, holding the woman so she does not fall during this movement; and if the hands still cannot be drawn in, and the child is dead, then sever its hands with the knife that was described before, extract it, and reset as evenly as possible.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	On the birth of the child on its feet.
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut; et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz; puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	When the child is born on its feet, one must push it upwards; and then turn it over repeatedly until it is level; then take one foot and stretch it gently.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi; si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	Once it reaches the thighs, command him to grab hold, and make him sneeze vigorously; if he jumps up, so be it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if he does not jump as we have said, turn him over repeatedly until he is in his natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then he will be lightly born.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier; et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz; et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre; puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	And if he does not come forth as we have said, take a mixture of musk root, almond oil, and melted gum, grind all together in a mortar; and place this ointment on the woman's nature inside and outside, then make her sit in tepid water up to below the ribs; and when she is softened below, make a myrrh collar for her, and put it underneath, leave it there an hour; then make her sit upon a stool, then make her sneeze, hold her mouth and nose shut, gently press on her belly, for now the child jumps.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	On the birth of a child on their knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc; puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit; et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval; et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains; et ewe l’enfant poc et poc; et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	When the child arrives in this form, place the midwife's hands there and there; then let her put her hand on his neck, and hang the baby's feet down, and let him lie on the bed; fold his hands there and there, and take the midwife's hands to press on the belly, and remove the pillows from under it until she is prepared below; if he does not cry out, then grasp his feet firmly, then move the stomach up, then put forth all of your hands; deliver the child there and there; tell the mother to hold herself while the baby emerges.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	On the birth of a child with an arm protruding from the wide passage
I covient engignier a ramener la main: s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler; s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment; puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit; et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main; et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	I must help to draw back the arm: if you cannot do it, make her stand up and walk; if she can't walk, then have her lie on the bed with legs raised high; bring out the midwife's kit as I described; if she still does not give birth, place her on a seat, then try to pull back the hand; deliver the baby naturally according to its position, make her sneeze, and tell her to hold herself until the child is born.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the exit of the child upon its neck, and have spread out his hands, and his face turned towards the back of his mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement; et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc; et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	I agree that the physician should hold his hand, then turn it back and forth, and gently raise it; and when it is equalized, apply a natural poultice of alum and oil, as we have said, then instruct her to move it little by little; and once you have done this, make her sit on a chair, and command her to grasp it; and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In the same manner for all secondary dislocations.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie; et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes; puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois: adonques si istra legierement.	When it happens forcefully in this manner for all secondary dislocations, scoop the moisture with your nail until it is emptied; and if the child falls on its face or neck, scoop them from under his nose so they are not obstructed, and clear the child; then push the child inside, until you have placed him correctly, and command the woman to grasp herself once: then gently extract.
de l’issue des gemelz	Of the dislocation of the knees
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four are born; and this is not a strange occurrence, it happens often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom; je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude; et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	Such are strange occurrences, and they do not live, if born prematurely; I know this, that they be multiplied, and are separated by the surgeon who divides them, which is tied to fate; and sometimes they are also born naturally like a single child, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait; et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	And if they are born prematurely, treat them as we have said, and let the midwife be skilled, and act swiftly and gently in what she does; and do so for their well-being.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient; si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	None of the times are formed in the marriage I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or many up to XV, and they are all shaped as children by the measurement of the glorious blood, and it is necessary that the bailiff knows everything, for perhaps similar things happen to him; he should act accordingly.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains; si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort; si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees; et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant; puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges; puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief; si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes; et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide; et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	When you treat the woman for a dead child in her belly, as I said in the previous division, and there is no delivery of the child, and you have to perform manual labor; it is necessary that you know if the woman is virtuous, and has not had any accidents or fears death. The woman should be positioned on her back with her legs lifted, and a minister should hold her mouth open with moist oils mixed with a poultice of althea, fenugreek, and flax seeds, then anoint your hands with these oils and poultices; gently insert them into the womb, until you feel where to position the hooks. Take care if the child is equipped that it descends onto its head; place the hooks in its eyes, neck, mouth, palate, under the beard, or near the armpits, and if the descent is through the feet, hook it by the heel and lower abdomen. You must hold the hook with your right hand and put the curve between two fingers of your left hand, then gently insert it completely into one of these places that we have mentioned until you reach an empty space; this is how the hook should look like:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz; et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	Then insert it against another clamp, or the third if you need them, so that the extractions are equal; and then extend them evenly by moving from one side to the other, to remove (the arrow), and let the clamps be toothed to hold it firmly, as follows:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie; et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if a part of it remains, oil your hands with some oil and push in that part, then pull the other part; and if there are no points left, place this clamp above, and do so until it comes out entirely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote; puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	If one hand comes before the other and you cannot pull it back due to constriction, then you must wrap it in a cloth until it is all covered; then cut at the joint of the palm or near the wrist, and do likewise with the other hand and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue; ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui; et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment; et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer; et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues; et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if the child's head is large and it is stuck during birth, or there is an acute assembly at the crown, you must place the pointed forceps between your fingers, split open the head, and extract the infant; or use the instrument called "almidach", from which its form comes with instruments described in this chapter; do the same if the child has a large natural head; then pull out the bones with tongs, and if the head is released by force and it tightens again, it should be cut open until the moist tissue that was at the narrow passage is exposed; if it cannot come out, sever it into pieces as far as you can reach; and if it swells in the belly or beneath the ribs, you must pierce it there so that the tissue flows.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is standing on their feet, then the traction is light, and the correction towards the mouth of the uterus is also light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main; et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre; et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris; puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer; et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses; et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	If it is trapped in the belly or hips, you must extract it with cloth wrapped around your hand; and split open the belly or hips until the moisture that is there comes out; and if other parts are removed but the head remains, place your hand over the uterus and draw it towards the mouth of the uterus; then insert one or two fingers and push them inwards; and if the mouth of the uterus is narrow due to a hot abscess which has formed there, you must not work it, instead apply moist and oily things; use poultices for this, and also soak with softeners that are wet and softening.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif; et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if the child is lying on its side, and you can position it evenly, then apply what we have described for a living infant; but if one has no power over this, then pull him apart by pieces, leaving nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris; et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	Once you have done this, then apply what we have described for hot abscesses that come to the surface; and if there is an outflow of blood, it should be immersed in cold water, restraining it, and other treatments will follow.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly a child had died, then another one grew on top of it, and the other died as well.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came to the navel, swelling until it opened up, and began with great suppuration.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat him, and I thought long about it, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster of strong attraction, and an [first] bone came out, after some days another one did too.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly astonished for there is no bone in the belly.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it might be bones from a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point; et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu; et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	I opened the wound and pulled out several bones, so that the woman was in a better condition; she lived for some time like this with only a little bowels missing from the place [where they had been], but I have not recorded this chapter except to show that when masters find strange cases, they should know how to treat them.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring the marrow to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	Here is the form of the pressor, to which one owes the ligaments; and turning back to the second shoulder joint.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux; et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi; et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus; et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	However, the horns should be more slender than those of the restrictor, and they should be made of ebony or boxwood; and the opening in the trunk should be two fingers wide, and the width between the trees is one finger; and at midpoint between the two ligaments are two fittings from this same wood, which are securely attached to each other, having a length of half a palm or slightly more; and these two fittings are pushed into the opening of the marrow to open when you turn the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles; et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large; et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes; puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Another form, similar but more slender and lighter, should be made of ebony or boxwood wood like a pair of tongs; and at the two shoulders it has two fittings, as you see, one palm long and two fingers wide; and when you wish to open the marrow with this whole instrument, have the woman sit on a bed, feet hanging down and legs apart, then insert the two fitted parts together into the marrow, hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs; next operate your hand on the whole instrument as you did with the tongs equally, according to the amount that you wish to open the mouth of the marrow until the baby does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all improved upon and their designs multiplied; when the surgeon has prepared them, his work is more efficient and of higher quality to men for their benefit.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Despair not over the instrument you lack, for its necessity is no excuse.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis; et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	When the midwife is held back from childbirth, instruct the patient to hold her breath and then make her sneeze violently, pressing your hands over her mouth and nose; if she faints due to this, it will be for the best.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire; toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	If not, take a pot and pierce the lid with holes, placing herbs within it to open up her mouth such as nettle, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia and centaury; cook these herbs or some of them in water over fire, then place one end of the pipe into the perforated pot and insert the other end inside the mouth of the patient, holding this until vapours enter her body; next make her sneeze as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the nurse's aid fails.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction; mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	And if the nurse remains after this treatment and does not leave promptly, instruct her to wet her left hand in oil of sesame or muskroot juice, then insert it into the vagina and grasp the child; when she finds it, grab it and stretch it little by little directly, so that the husband does not hinder its extraction; but she must move it gently right and left, then pull; thus it will come out and disengage.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes; et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire; mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon; si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	And if the mouth of the womb is narrowed, we have mentioned the treatment of sneezing and herb fumigation; and if it does not respond to all that we have said, beware that you do not force extraction; but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the womb should be tied to the thigh of the woman, then she must be clystered with four-ingredient ointment; this will ripen and reset it, and it will come out; however, when it rips, a bad smell comes from the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	So befits then appropriate fumigations for this: some of the ancients have tried using cress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman for retention of her flowers and menstruum is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu; et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And it is of glass similar to a bowl, and one puts the skilled head inside, and the wide ends over the fire; and let the fumigation be above the coals, and leave until wasted, then begin another.
de percier lou fondement	To perforate the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac: si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche; puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many children are born without a perforated fundament, instead having it stuffed with a skilled plug: so one must at bathing pierce this plug for them, and not use a pointed spatula, taking care that they do not touch it; then place moist wool soaked in wine and oil upon it, then treat with ointment until healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not heal, place a cork stopper in the hole, and leave it for several days; remove it when the child wants to go outside.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	Sometimes this closure occurs suddenly in a wound or abscess; so it is necessary to cut through the sudden blockage: it should be treated as we said for the cork stopper.
de la fistule dou fondement	Of the anal fistula.
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	Anal fistulas that originate beneath the anus are nodules and growths, which come from outside or in the space between the two parts; if there is one or more fistula with old nodules, it can be operated on and even moist white worms or fine worms come out; sometimes these fistulas are penetrating, and they are known by those who have them through egestion or flatulence when the patient defecates, and perhaps some worms fall out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if there are fistulas that reach up to the bladder and up to half of the penis's length; they may also extend to the hip joint and even down to the knee cap.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant: et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	Hereby we identify the fistula penetrating anus and not penetrating; for this, insert your index finger into the anus and push a fine needle of brass or iron inside the fistula where it is not tortuous.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit; et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit: saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	And if there is tortuosity, insert a slender tent of lead or horsehair until you feel the tent or hair with your finger; and if you do not feel it, and from the opening no feces nor wind come out as we said before: know that it does not pierce; so hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has penetrated up to the bladder or up to the urinary duct, thus letting out urine, it cannot be healed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu; s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement; et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	If it has perforated up to the hip joint, then the ulcer will also reach that place; if there is no tortuosity and the pain is felt around it, then one should wait for it to improve on its own, and medicine or ointment are not effective in healing this immediately; regarding these penetrating fistulas, there is nothing else other than hard work, and the folly of foolish surgeons who get involved.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre; puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	In the case of one that is not penetrated and is not old, there is hope for recovery through iron instruments, as I have experienced; it is such that the patient lies between your hands on his back; you lift his legs until they reach his hips, and incline his hips towards his stomach; then insert a copper probe or tin if there is tortuosity, until you know where the ulcer comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans; si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If the patient feels it around the anus, you must insert your index finger there; if you then feel that the tendon has been pierced; and if what you sense between your finger and the skin or flesh is uncovered, know that it is perforated; do not labor here for one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc; et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit; et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil; et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	One says however that one can indeed heal some of these, but it happens rarely; and the aid given here, consists in heating the fine cauterizer according to the width of the fistula as said before; and insert it all hot into the fistula until you reach near the anus; do this two or three times so that you know that the faulty flesh is burned which resembles a bird's feather; then treat it with wet bandages in butter, until that flesh be gone, and finally dress it with healing ointment softening the flesh and welding.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus cured, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez; et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur; si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente; et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	If this cannot be cured in any other way, and if it enters but does not penetrate all the way to the rectum, and between your finger and the fistula is a thick covering of flesh or skin, and you see the opening on the surface of the cover; then cut from the beginning of the fistula and push forward with the tent, and cauterize afterward until you reach the head of the tent. The tent will be relieved and fall out, and beware not to damage those faulty tissues that look like feathers, and leave nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if blood defeats you and escapes between your finger and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or astringent medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor; puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe; puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	For cauterization with fire combines two beneficial effects: namely, the burning of adjacent flesh and the stemming of blood flow along with drying up moisture; then treating damp wounds with butter or pulverized substances until the wound produces little discharge and the burnt flesh turns white; afterwards cure the injury with ointments that induce scabs on hardening rough skin, which are dry medications.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	When it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula reaches up to the anus, and is far from the body, insert your finger into the anus, and feel for it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres: ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit; puis le cure, si com nos avons dit; par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé; puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues; puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If you feel the tumor, and between it are either membranes or sinews or flesh, where it is close to breaking through, do not despair that there is no hope unless one of three methods is applied: cauterize as we have mentioned, or cut down deeply, or if you can apply an ointment and treat as initially; be careful not to cut too deep into the wall which supports the anus, lest waste come out involuntarily; then cure it as said before; perhaps this will heal, or remove that covering and clean once it is cut away from the anus, either with an ointment or another pointed instrument; thereafter soften that hardened flesh which remains in the injury as much as you can; finally treat the wound, and prevent the fistula's return to the area beyond the anus: this would be less onerous for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	And sometimes fistulas are formed in this manner: it is when you insert a probe into the fistula, and it lies close to the base of the fundament near the skin above, take a perforated probe with a pointed end in this shape:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And here you insert the thread awry into it [the probe], and insert the probe along the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement; et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II; et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent; puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	If it perforates the margin of the fundament inside, then withdraw the thread from that hole, just as you would insert your finger into the fundament; and draw out the tip of the thread, and bring together the two ends, pressing one against the other, and leave them there for one or two days; press [the thread] sometimes so that it grips those parts which are between the two [ends], and closes [the fistula]; then treat the wound until it is healed and closed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not break open, make it do so by all means possible if it is not too deeply embedded.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not appropriate to remove what is too deeply embedded by suturing, and then treat it as we have said until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans; et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	The shape of the spinal needle used to create a fistula is very sharp on one side and blunt on the other so that you do not cut what must not be cut as you can see here:
des emorroydes	Of hemorrhoids.
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors; et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz; si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines; et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot; et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere; ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez; et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement; cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere; et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	Hemorrhoids are of two types: they can be found inside the anus like resin grains and come in small or large sizes; they also bleed and may appear singly or in groups, and they emerge from outside the anus at its beginning but those that do have little moisture with some light yellow liquid or a bit of blood; their color matches that of the body. The cure for these types which are found inside the anus is to instruct the patient to strain themselves so as to evacuate their bowels until the hemorrhoids emerge from it, then you hasten and use forceps or hold them with your nail before cutting at its root; if they cannot be held by forceps due to moisture, take a piece of linen, cotton, or chamois leather and extract them using both hands then cut them off, apply hot powder over them as would be done for cauterization according to the chapter on cautery. You can treat them with other treatments until it is healed; if the anus cannot be evacuated, administer the patient a bitter enema that is rough so as to wash out what is inside the anus so it may come out naturally. When patients push hard and these hemorrhoids are outside of the anus then treatment becomes less invasive: take them with your nail or forceps and cut them off before treating them in the way we have mentioned until they heal, and fear incisions made by iron instruments.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc; puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose; et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If you must treat the wound, it's best to do so in this way: take a straight thread and insert it into a needle; pass the end of the thread through the needle from below upward; then turn back both ends of the thread under the needle so that they are parallel with each other. Tie the thread firmly, remove the needle and repeat for all areas requiring stitches; leave one stitch untied to allow drainage of excess blood; place over this a piece of linen cloth moistened in rose oil or cerate, then replace it over the wound and tell the patient to rest until bleeding has stopped completely; cure them with ointments and other treatments so that they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	the drying out of faeces or the fundament 
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is constipation in the intestine, caused by the constraint of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine fails to work.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir; puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient; et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez; puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	You should remove the bark with a spatula or your nail at the point of a sputum ulcer, ensuring it doesn't become moist; then treat it until it is firm as required; and if it cannot heal, increase the strength of the scraping until it heals significantly, and becomes scarred; then treat it again until it is healed.
dou fremit	How it itches.
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont; et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	Formice is a small faulty appearance within the body, which spreads rapidly; sometimes it finds cold and feels just like an itch, spreading throughout the entire body, but more so in the hands than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor; puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	And the cure is that you take a cane made from a goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and place this cane on the trembling, so that the purple circles touch the trembling all around; then turn your hand over the entire cane such that you cover the trembling all around it, and insert it perfectly, extracting the tremor from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, make something similar with a brass or iron cane according to this form, and let it be subtle below and straight above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce it, in order to hold it with your fingers, and squeeze it; And if you wish, cauterize the tremor, as described before in the chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	Of the form of an enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Never make an enema of silver or quicksilver, or of molten and strained brass; nor should any of these instruments be made small or large, according to what they are adapted for.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those which are used in the treatment of children who are feeble and afflicted should be small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema is broad above, where the bellies are fastened according to this method:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I; et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre; et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And there is a release where the bellies are fastened, as you see, and the head is pierced inside it; and have on one side two holes, and on the other one; and let the belly in which the medicine is placed be made of the bladder of an animal or parchment, and pierced all around with small holes, and between each hole there should be a space of one inch, then push into these holes a strong thread of spun linen twisted crosswise in the form of an X or otherwise round, and sew up the belly like a goat; and when the medicine is inside it, bind it to the instrument before with a strong thread, then enema; and this is the form of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement; puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And let the medicament be neither too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the catheter with oil or egg white, or something similar, then insert it gently; then have the ministers squeeze with both hands together until everything is out, then remove the catheter, and raise the patient's legs to the wall, and if the medic wants to evacuate, let them as much as they can; and if he sleeps a night through, so much the better.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you catheterize him for the disease of abdominal prolapse, and the medicament comes out quickly, repeat it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And if the hemorrhoids are at the anus or abscess, let the catheter be as gentle as for a child; and this is the form of the gentle catheter with which the skin is tightened:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already spoken about the treatment of wounds in the previous section; now we will discuss the cures and medicines according to their application.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, where the wound is located, and what caused it.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses; ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres; et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	Wounds are caused by various things such as stone impacts, sword or knife cuts, lance or stick injuries, arrows, and similar objects; they can also be classified based on the body part affected, like wounds on the neck, head, foot, stomach, liver, and other similar areas of the body. I will tell you about the treatment for each type of wound, starting with simple head wounds since their treatment methods will be discussed in detail later.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree; et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	I say that when a simple wound occurs on the head, and the bone is not broken, take note if it is due to a blow from a stone or similar objects, and the skin is still torn with a large wound, and you have slight doubts about an incipient abscess: then cause the patient to bleed soon through the cephalic vein especially if little blood comes out of the wound, and let this bleeding be on the opposite side of the injured part; and let the sick person abstain from food and heavy meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char; et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice; et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés; et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he does not want to bleed, then let his diet be reduced, and let him drink no wine, nor eat any meat; and put on the wound, if hot abscesses appear, moist cotton soaked in rose oil only, or with astringent wine; and if there is no hot abscess, then apply to the wound, while it is fresh and full of blood, and has not been moved by air, powder which I will mention a little later; and if the air has moved it, then put on some ointments until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	Et if the wound is large like a sword cut or similar, and the lips cannot be brought together with sutures, then they are joined by stitching, as I will explain for wounds of the belly, regarding suturing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	If the wound is exposed down to the bone, gaping, and holds only by a point, then it should be amputated; afterward treat the wound with medicine, restore hard flesh in place of the skin, and instruct the patient to eat coarse meats like beef or pork, as well as grains such as wheat, boiled peas, chicken, and similar foods.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure; et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil; et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if you find that the skin is festering but it has not reached bone then cut away all the rotten tissue and discard it, afterward treat the wound with medicine; should there be an artery in the wound or vein that does not stop bleeding even after applying medicines bind it off, and if you find it severed tie it up with a thread; if this brings no benefit cauterize the area.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light: it is necessary that you apply this powder which will heal as soon as the ointment has moved.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon II parties; chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc; et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	The manner of the powder is as follows: take one part incense; two parts dragon's blood; three parts quicklime, and finely grind the powder, then apply it to the wound, pressing firmly until it dries well and joins with all its blood; then bind it tightly, and leave it without loosening, if there is no swelling; for you remove the medicine only when it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes you only use the quicklime when you lack incense or dragon's blood, but let the ointment heal the wound first.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre; mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe; puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the fire has caused movement in the wound, especially during summer, do not apply this powder but use some soothing ointments or poultices made from barley flour with water and honey until it flows freely; then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz; et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	And if the bone fracture occurs with the wound, and it is minor, extract it using subtle pincers; I will tell you about skull fractures later.
de la plaie dou col	On the neck wound
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is straightforward, there is no significant difference between this and a skull fracture; however, if the carotid artery or jugular vein in the neck has been severed.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire; et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres; mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	If it is the black eye, there is no other treatment but to let it heal, and put nothing constricting on it, for it harms the eye and makes it withdraw; and do not apply anything cold to the wound, because the substance of the eyes is cold, and its connection is with the brain, which is the highest organ; but use a soothing medicine, such as lukewarm wash in warm water, and mixed with rose oil, and cooked leek washed also in warm water, and other stones of similar nature, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, cut it and bind with bandages, then treat it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu; et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est; et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel; et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez; et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier; et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue; et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.
