Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	When it is fully dislocated, you must have the patient sit straight, and hold their ministers aside with one hand by the leg, above the ankle; then draw the foot towards yourself with your right hand, and twice to the left, then stretch it upwards, and push the foot upwards gently; do this twice, as we have said, pushing and drawing the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, begin the work again, for it will return; and if it cannot be returned thus, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly insert a stick into the earth between their thighs, tying the cloth around it so that it does not hurt the patient; then have one minister hold the thigh, while another stretches the foot with their hands or a cord tied above the ankle; both ministers should stretch equally, and let the stick be held between the patient's thighs to steady them when they are stretched; then place the healers' hands evenly on the dislocation, while another minister holds the healthy leg underneath, and the dislocation will return speedily.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is at the right point, apply the plaster and pads on top, pressing firmly, and bind the foot to the leg, taking care that the ligaments above the ankle from behind are not too tight; then leave it for two or three days, if the binding loosens, press again; then release it on the third or fourth day, and prevent the patient from walking for four days; and if they walk before this term is over, it is not safe that it will dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if hot abscesses appear there, you must treat them as we have said elsewhere until they are healed.
des dois	twice.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the thumb is dislocated, it should be gently stretched without work, and this is an easy matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any of the joints of the foot or back, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or a straight table, and place your foot on what appears to be these joints, then press firmly with your foot until it returns; once it is aligned and nothing seems amiss, place beneath the sole of their foot a two-foot long board, strain them firmly, and leave them for three days; afterwards, undo the bandage, and let them rest until they heal.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wounds and dislocations together:
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound occurs alongside a dislocation and one wishes to restore it, many times the patient dies: do not be presumptuous in your cure if you are not wise in this art and have long practiced it, and if you are not merciful and compassionate; and use at first soothing remedies for hot abscesses, leaving the patient in God's hands should you see no hope of health; but when there is a chance of healing, restore now the limb to its place even though hot abscesses may arise; once the limb is restored, administer soothing medicines for hot abscesses and treat the wound as befits it with drying ointments; if alongside the dislocation there are broken bones or small pieces of bone displaced, remove them, and do what we have said in simple illnesses; take care to not fall into fear's path, according to what I've said, because this will lead you astray from your Creator, and towards harm for both your soul and body.
Amen	Amen
